2004-07-14: marcel@hsdev.com: ChangeSet 1.1849.14.12
  New custom command which lists the authors of a file, this will help us with the copyright transferSyntax:bk authors        - list all authors in the repositorybk authors <file> - lists the authors for the particular fileThe command uses a file BitKeeper/custom/author_map to map bitkeepers idea of users to Real Life names. If none is found, the bitkeeper name is used.Once the repository is converted into copyright clean, a trigger will be installed which checks in real time whether the Real Name of a committer can be found, so we always know which real name corresponds to a certain bk name.

2004-04-05: ccorliss@lxwdev-1.schwabfoundation.org: ChangeSet 1.1815.47.5
  xarDB.php:  fix for bug #2644ADODB currently allows setting of fetch mode via global and the method setfetchmode()however, it doesn't seem to take into account the global setting when setfetchmode is setwhich causes problems in postgres drivers (and possibly others). reason being that these drivers,don't actually use the setFetchMode method everywhere - instead opting for the global (which can be out of sync with the latter).
